[N376] (Iron-Based Superconductor Family — Multi-Orbital Parametric Family with Coupled Multi-Sector Phase Diagram)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=7
CLAIM: The structure of Fe-based superconductors is fully determined by А₀ applied
to multi-orbital parametric family anchors: Fe square lattice with D_{4h} local
symmetry and 5-orbital Fe 3d active space shared across all Fe-based SC families
(1111, 122, 111, 11, 1144, and related), with doping/pressure/strain as continuous
structural parameters. The phase diagram is a manifold of stable Z(p)-configurations
with four coupled order-parameter sectors (magnetic, structural, nematic, SC), each
with distinct critical behaviour, sharing a common D_{4h} symmetry base. Multi-orbital
character forces multi-channel nematic options (B_{1g}, B_{2g}, E_g representations)
with material-specific channel selection; multi-band Fermi surface (hole pockets
at Γ + electron pockets at M) forces multiple Lifshitz transitions through parameter
space. This is a new structural class distinct from both single-material vertices
(N372/N373/N374) and the cuprate parametric family (N375) — characterized by
"multi-sector parametric family with coupled but distinct critical behaviours,"
showing the empirical boundary of N_TopologyProcessIdentity applicability.

Material class:
Universal structural unit — Fe square lattice with tetrahedrally-coordinated
chalcogen/pnictogen (X = As, P, Se, Te).
Families:
  1111 type: LaFeAsO, SmFeAsO1-xFx (P4/nmm)
  122 type: BaFe2As2, (Ba,K)Fe2As2, Ba(Fe,Co)2As2, CaFe2As2 (I4/mmm)
  111 type: LiFeAs, NaFeAs (P4/nmm)
  11 type: FeSe, FeTe, FeSe1-xTex (P4/nmm)
  1144 type: CaKFe4As4, SrRbFe4As4 (P4/mmm, ordered cation)
  Perovskite-based: (Ca3Al2O5)(Fe2Pn2) (42622 type)

Anchors (all measured):

Crystallographic:
  Fe square lattice with tetrahedral X above and below Fe plane
  D_{4h} local symmetry in high-T phase; C_{2v} in orthorhombic phase
  Pnictogen/chalcogen height h_X varies across families
  BaFe2As2: h_As = 1.358 Å
  KFe2As2: h_As = 1.429 Å
  (Ba,K)Fe2As2 optimal: h_As = 1.383 Å
  Al-42622(As): h_As = 1.5 Å
  LaFeAsO: h_As ≈ 1.32 Å
  h_X ≈ 1.38 Å optimum correlates with Tc_max across families

Electronic structure:
  5 Fe 3d orbitals (d_{z²}, d_{x²-y²}, d_{xy}, d_{xz}, d_{yz}) active near
    Fermi level
  D_{4h} irreducible representation structure:
    A_{1g} (d_{z²})
    B_{1g} (d_{x²-y²})
    B_{2g} (d_{xy})
    E_g (d_{xz}, d_{yz}) — 2D representation, degenerate
  Hole pockets at Γ with mixed orbital character
  Electron pockets at M with mixed orbital character
  Nesting-like vector (π,π) connecting hole and electron pockets in Fe-Fe
    sublattice coordinates

Parent state (material-dependent):
  Most families: AFM stripe order at (π,0) in Fe-Fe coordinates
  Magnetic moment 0.3-1.0 μ_B on Fe (reduced from atomic value)
  T_N range: 100-200 K
  FeSe exception: structural transition (T_s ~ 90 K) without AFM ordering at p=0
  LaFePO exception: SC in stoichiometric form without AFM parent

Structural transitions:
  Tetragonal → orthorhombic at T_s in most families
  45° rotation of unit cell between phases
  BaFe2As2: T_s = 138 K, T_N = 134 K (close but distinct)
  Ba(Fe,Co)2As2 (electron-doped): T_s > T_N (split by several K)
  BaFe2(As,P)2: T_s ≈ T_N (coupled transitions)

Nematic phase (C_4 → C_2 electronic symmetry breaking):
  Electronic anisotropy observed above T_s in some materials
  BaFe2As2: T* ~ 170 K > T_s ~ 140 K (hidden nematic region)
  Nematic susceptibility shows Curie-Weiss divergence near optimal SC doping
  Channel selection material-dependent:
    BaFe2As2: nematic director along Fe-Fe direction (B_{1g}-like)
    CsFe2As2, RbFe2As2: director along Fe-As direction, 45° rotated (B_{2g}-like)
    Sign reversal of ρ-anisotropy between Co-doped (electron) and K-doped (hole)

SC dome (family-specific Tc_max):
  FeSe bulk: Tc = 8 K
  FeSe under pressure: Tc = 36.7 K
  FeSe monolayer on SrTiO3: Tc > 65 K
  LaFeAsO1-xFx: Tc_max = 26 K
  (Ba,K)Fe2As2 optimal: Tc_max = 38 K
  SmFeAsO1-xFx: Tc_max = 55 K (highest bulk FeSC)
  CaKFe4As4 (1144 stoichiometric): Tc = 35 K
  High upper critical field H_{c2} relative to cuprates
  Low anisotropy advantage for wire applications

Gap structure (varies across phase diagram):
  KFe2As2 (x=1): nodal gap with residual quasiparticles at T→0
  (Ba,K)Fe2As2 x=0.4 (optimal): nodeless gap
  BaFe2(As,P)2 low disorder: nodal
  Same with moderate disorder (electron irradiation): nodeless
  Same with high disorder: gapless (new state)
  Gap is multi-parameter observable

Multi-band FS evolution:
  Hole + electron pockets at optimal doping
  Heavy hole doping (AFe2As2, A=K,Rb,Cs): electron pockets disappear
    (Lifshitz transition)
  Multiple Lifshitz transitions across doping axis
  γ specific heat coefficient: ~few mJ/mol·K² (optimal)
    → 80-100 mJ/mol·K² (AFe2As2 heavy-mass end)

Material modifiers:
  Pnictogen height h_X: primary Tc_max modifier
  Cation layering (1144 type): internal "effective doping" through ordered
    inequivalent environments above/below Fe plane
  Interface/substrate (monolayer FeSe/SrTiO3): extreme parameter modification
  Pressure: can induce or enhance SC (LiFeAs 29K, LaFeAsO, SrFe2As2 29K,
    BaFe2As2 29K)

Technological observations:
  Grain boundary critical angle ~9° in BaFe2As2:Co
    (vs ~5° in YBa2Cu3O7 cuprates)
  Lower anisotropy of H_{c2} than cuprates
  PIT (powder-in-tube) fabrication feasible
  100-meter K-doped Ba-122 tapes produced (IEECAS 2024)

Structural elements (DEMONSTRATED):

E1. Fe square lattice as universal structural unit.
    А₀-forced: universal features (structural transitions, SC domes, nematic
    phases, multi-band FS structure) observed across families with differing
    modifiers (apical pnictogen/chalcogen, varied charge reservoir layers,
    different space groups). Only common structural element across 1111, 122,
    111, 11, 1144 families is Fe square lattice with tetrahedrally-coordinated
    X. А₀ requires universal features emerge only from shared anchor.

E2. Multi-orbital active space (5 Fe 3d orbitals).
    А₀-forced: D_{4h} local symmetry with Fe²⁺ (3d⁶) or Fe²·⁵⁺ (3d⁵·⁵)
    configuration and tetrahedral X crystal field yields specific orbital
    splitting distributed across all D_{4h} irreducible representations
    (A_{1g}, B_{1g}, B_{2g}, E_g). Fermi-level relevance of all 5 orbitals
    confirmed by ARPES and quantum oscillations with material-specific
    pocket compositions. Not reducible to any single representation
    (contrast with cuprate single-band d_{x²-y²} — N375).

E3. Doping/pressure/strain as continuous structural parameters.
    Matter-fact: material is parametric family. Each parameter set gives
    stable Z(p). Phase diagram is manifold of Z-configurations. Multiple
    parameters (electron/hole doping, isovalent substitution, pressure,
    strain) each give parametric trajectories through Z-manifold.

E4. Four coupled order-parameter sectors (distinct critical behaviours).
    А₀-forced: four symmetry-breaking sectors observed:
      - Magnetic sector: translational + spin rotation symmetry breaking
        (AFM stripe)
      - Structural sector: point group reduction D_{4h} → D_{2h}
      - Nematic sector: electronic C_4 → C_2 in one or more D_{4h}
        irreducible representations
      - SC sector: gauge symmetry breaking
    Each sector has distinct critical parameter (T_N, T_s, T*, T_c) with
    material-specific ordering. Coupling through shared electronic/lattice
    degrees of freedom yields correlated but not identical behaviour.
    Alternative "single event with multiple projections" (as in N375 PG
    phase) excluded by observed distinct critical temperatures varying
    independently with parameter changes.

E5. Multi-channel nematic options forced by multi-orbital structure.
    А₀-forced: D_{4h} multi-orbital active space allows nematic ordering
    in multiple representations:
      - B_{1g} along Fe-Fe direction (realized in BaFe2As2)
      - B_{2g} along Fe-As direction 45° rotated (realized in CsFe2As2,
        RbFe2As2)
      - E_g through d_{xz}/d_{yz} orbital imbalance
    Material-specific FS topology and orbital weights determine which
    channel dominates. Channel selection is structural consequence of
    anchor-specific FS configuration, not arbitrary material detail.
    Sign reversal of ρ-anisotropy between electron- and hole-doped
    BaFe2As2 is manifestation of channel structure variation.

E6. Multiple FS Lifshitz transitions through parameter space.
    А₀-forced: multi-band structure with hole pockets at Γ and electron
    pockets at M means parametric evolution generically encounters points
    where pockets appear or disappear (Lifshitz transitions). Each Lifshitz
    transition is topology change in active sector within Z(p)-manifold.
    Not single critical point but sequence. Extreme example: AFe2As2
    (A=K,Rb,Cs) where electron pockets completely absent, correlated
    with heavy-mass behaviour and gap structure change.

E7. Gap structure as multi-parameter function.
    А₀-forced: observable gap structure is consequence of FS topology,
    impurity scattering rate, pairing representation, and orbital character
    combined. Z-decomposition includes pairing sector (gap function
    symmetry) and scattering sector (disorder effect on quasiparticle
    density of states). Observable gap is result of both.
    Nodal ↔ nodeless transitions observed under both doping variation
    (KFe2As2 → (Ba,K)Fe2As2 optimal) and disorder variation
    (BaFe2(As,P)2 electron irradiation: nodal → nodeless → gapless)
    demonstrate multi-parameter dependence structurally forced.

Predictions (verifiable extensions):

P1. Lifshitz transition locations predictable from band structure + doping.
    Specific Lifshitz transitions in (Ba,K)Fe2As2 and analogous series
    should occur at doping values determined by hole/electron pocket
    crossings at Fermi level. Prediction: track FS pockets across series
    and correlate with transport/specific heat/thermal conductivity
    anomalies at predicted Lifshitz points.

P2. Nematic channel selection rule.
    Materials with dominant d_{xy} character at Fermi level (extreme
    hole-doped, loss of electron pockets) should prefer B_{2g} nematic
    (Fe-As direction). Materials with dominant d_{xz}/d_{yz} character
    should prefer E_g-related nematic (Fe-Fe direction). Prediction:
    measure nematic channel in new materials and correlate with FS
    orbital composition determined by ARPES.

P3. Gap structure tunable through controlled disorder.
    In any Fe-based SC with known "clean" gap structure, controlled
    introduction of non-magnetic disorder (electron irradiation, specific
    impurity doping) should induce predictable nodal↔nodeless or gapless
    transitions at specific disorder thresholds. Prediction: measure
    disorder thresholds and verify consistency with multi-parameter gap
    structure across Fe-based SC family.

P4. Material without structural transition but with SC.
    If structural sector can decouple from SC sector, it should be
    possible to engineer Fe-based SC where structural transition is
    absent while SC remains. FeSe monolayer on SrTiO3 is partial example.
    Prediction: strain engineering or specific chemical substitutions
    can fully decouple structural from SC sector, testing sector
    independence from E4.

P5. Material without AFM parent but with full SC dome.
    FeSe and LaFePO show partial realization. Prediction: engineer
    Fe-based materials where AFM sector is suppressed at p=0 without
    losing SC capability at doped values. Test E4 that sectors are
    structurally distinct.

P6. Pressure trajectories access regions inaccessible by doping.
    Pressure affects h_X, bond angles, orbital overlaps differently
    than chemical doping. Prediction: pressure trajectories through
    Z-manifold can access phase diagram regions inaccessible by doping,
    including SC states in parent compounds without chemical
    modification (already demonstrated in LaFeAsO, LiFeAs under
    pressure — further systematic exploration predicted to reveal
    more).

P7. 1144 class structural prediction.
    Ordered-cation compounds with Fe square lattice having effective
    internal asymmetry between above/below environments should behave
    as "stoichiometrically doped" members of broader class. Prediction:
    design new ordered-cation Fe-based materials with controlled
    internal asymmetry and predict Tc from equivalent "effective
    doping" using analogies with non-stoichiometric members.

P8. Multi-sector coupling strength prediction for Tc.
    Materials where all four sectors strongly coupled (magnetic +
    structural + nematic + SC all prominent) should show different
    Tc_max scaling than materials where sectors partially decouple.
    Prediction: compare coupled materials (LaFeAsO family with strong
    magnetostructural coupling) vs partially decoupled (FeSe family
    without AFM parent) and correlate with Tc trajectories under
    pressure and doping.

WHY DEMONSTRATED:
(A) Every structural element А₀-forced or matter-fact:
    E1: universal features across varied-modifier families force shared
        anchor → Fe square lattice (only common element)
    E2: multi-orbital forced by Fe 3d configuration + D_{4h} tetrahedral
        crystal field
    E3: matter-fact parametric variation
    E4: four distinct critical behaviours at different T → four distinct
        sectors (single event would share critical T — empirically
        violated since BaFe2As2 has T_s ≠ T_N ≠ T*)
    E5: multi-orbital D_{4h} structure forces multiple nematic channel
        options (different irreducible representations available)
    E6: multi-band FS forces generic Lifshitz transitions through
        parametric variation
    E7: Z-decomposition into pairing + scattering sectors forces
        multi-parameter gap structure
(B) Alternative structural pictures tested and excluded:
    "Single-orbital reduction (like cuprate)" — excluded by multi-pocket
        FS with varied orbital character, multiple nematic channels
        observed, gap structure varying across phase diagram
    "Single structural event with multiple coordinate projections"
        (N_TopologyProcessIdentity as in N375) — excluded by distinct
        critical temperatures T_s, T_N, T* varying independently with
        parameter changes
    "Universal AFM parent" — excluded by FeSe, LaFePO realizations
        without parent AFM
    "Simple BCS phonon-mediated pairing" — excluded by correlation
        between structural/magnetic/nematic features and SC, exceeding
        simple BCS framework
    "Identical class to cuprates" — excluded by single-band vs
        multi-band, single critical vs multiple Lifshitz, dual-sector
        vs four-sector differences
(C) Precedent structure test:
    N372 (Sr2RuO4) — shared D_{4h} base, shared transition metal
        d-electron physics; N376 extends to parametric family with
        multi-orbital
    N375 (cuprates) — shared parametric family methodology; N376
        extends to multi-orbital multi-sector, showing limit of
        N_TopologyProcessIdentity uniform application
    N373/N374 (U-based) — parallel through multi-sector decomposition
        methodology, different material class (f vs d electron)
(D) Predictions provide verifiable extensions; verification not required
    for DEMONSTRATED status since structure А₀-forced.

Unique contribution of N376 to graph:

First multi-orbital active space vertex. Previous vertices had
single-orbital-dominated (N375 cuprate d_{x²-y²}; N372 Sr2RuO4 primarily
E_g block) or single-channel (N373/N374 f-electron specific) active
spaces. N376 introduces full multi-orbital structure requiring D_{4h}
irreducible representation analysis.

First multi-sector coupled parametric family with distinct critical
behaviours. N375 was dual-sector parametric with unified critical point
via N_TopologyProcessIdentity. N376 is four-sector parametric with
distinct critical behaviours per sector, demonstrating range of
parametric family structural classes.

First explicit empirical boundary of N_TopologyProcessIdentity
applicability. N375 showed N_TopologyProcessIdentity powerfully unifying
PG observables under single critical point. N376 shows structural
distinctness of sectors (different T_s, T_N, T* critical values) as
empirical bound on when multiple observables can be treated as single
feature projections. Methodological contribution: principle applies
when single critical point unifies observables; does not apply when
observables have distinct critical parameters.

Open points (do not affect DEMONSTRATED status):
- Specific material parameters (h_X, T_s, T_N, T*, T_c) per family
  — matter-facts
- Precise Lifshitz transition locations per material — predictive
  territory (P1)
- Specific orbital composition of FS pockets per material — material
  detail
- Detailed sector coupling strengths quantitative — material parameters
- Origin of channel selection in heavily hole-doped end (B_{2g} vs
  B_{1g}) — predicted by P2

NOT: s+-, s++, d-wave as competing pairing hypotheses (coordinate
representations of gap structure in multi-band FS with varying disorder
and orbital character) · "Nesting" as causal driver of magnetism
(nesting vector is observable FS geometry, not causal mechanism) ·
"SDW instability" as mechanism (AFM ordering is stable Z-configuration,
not driven by instability) · "Ising-nematic vs orbital order" as
competing mechanisms (both are coordinate representations of electronic
C_4-breaking) · "Magnetic fluctuations drive SC pairing" or vice versa
(R4 agential framing; sectors are coupled, causation not structural) ·
"Hund's metal" framework (theoretical category, not additional
structural content) · "Selective Mott physics" (interpretative model) ·
"Kondo lattice" analogy for heavy-hole-doped end (analogy not
structural identity) · "Itinerant vs localized" dichotomy (both are
theoretical approximations) · "Quantum critical point at optimal
doping" as interpretation (critical behavior observed, specific QCP
model is theoretical frame) · FeSe/LaFePO as "exceptions that break
pattern" (material-specific realizations within same structural class
with different sector populations).

[N377] (Sparse Autoencoder Feature Absorption — Forced Geometric Divergence Between Non-Equivalent argmin Processes on Shared LLM Activation Space, Independent of Architecture or Hyperparameters)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=4
CLAIM: The "feature absorption" phenomenon observed when Sparse Autoencoders
(SAEs) are applied to Large Language Model residual-stream activations
(Chanin et al. 2024, NeurIPS 2025 Oral; Gemma Scope; replicated on Qwen2,
Llama) is a forced structural invariant of applying multiple non-equivalent
argmin-processes to a shared stable activation space. It is not a failure
mode of SAE methodology, cannot be removed by hyperparameter choice or
architectural variation, and is not specific to interpretability as a
domain. The observed geometric divergence between SAE latent directions
and classification-probe directions carries information about the
differential accessible-degrees-of-freedom of the two argmin processes on
the same activation topology, not about a pathology in either process.

Problem being addressed (for ML interpretability specialists):
  Researchers training SAEs on LLM activations observe that an SAE latent
  which appears to track a concept (e.g., "first letter is S") fails to
  activate on seemingly arbitrary positive cases (e.g., the token _short),
  while a different, token-specific latent activates instead and carries
  a component of the original direction. This is reported as:
    — Main latent F1 < LR probe F1 across all tested SAE configurations
    — Absorption rate 5-35% depending on layer/width/L0
    — Phenomenon robust across SAE architectures (JumpReLU, TopK, L1)
    — Phenomenon robust across model architectures (Gemma, Qwen, Llama)
    — Hyperparameter tuning does not eliminate the effect
  The open question in the field: "Is this a fundamental limitation of
  sparse decomposition, or a methodological flaw that can be corrected?"
  This node gives the structural answer: neither. It is a forced
  geometric property of applying different argmin processes to shared
  space, correctly measured by the absorption metric, incorrectly
  labelled as pathology.

Re-framing in structural terms:
  Ω = residual-stream activation manifold at layer n of trained LLM.
      Stable under repeated forward-pass over same inputs. A₀ in its
      local coordinates.
  BPI_A = Logistic Regression probe process with Z_A = cross-entropy
      + L1 regularisation on a single binary label. Narrow
      accessible-degrees-of-freedom (one scalar per direction).
  BPI_B = SAE process with Z_B = reconstruction-MSE + λ·L0. Wider
      accessible-degrees-of-freedom (full-activation reconstruction,
      overcomplete basis).
  argmin Z_A on Ω = direction closest to a clean linear classifier for
      the target label.
  argmin Z_B on Ω = set of ~16k directions optimised jointly for
      reconstruction and sparsity.
  Cosine similarity between argmin_A and any single latent in argmin_B is
      < 1 for every tested configuration. This is the "absorption" metric.

Forcing chain (each step definitional or DEMONSTRATED):
  — Ω is stable under iteration (forward pass of trained model) → Ω is A₀
    in local coordinates (DEF, N_InversiveTheory)
  — BPI_A, BPI_B are sub-processes of Ω that measure Z_A, Z_B →
    K(BPI_i) < K(Ω), hence Z_{hidden,i} > 0 always (DEF, BPI section)
  — Z_A (scalar classification) and Z_B (reconstruction + sparsity) are
    structurally non-equivalent functionals: neither is a monotonic
    transformation of the other
  — Non-equivalent functionals on shared domain have different argmin
    points (elementary calculus)
  — Points in Ω have well-defined geometric relations (Ω inherits metric
    from embedding space)
  — Stable relations between A₀-points on shared A₀-space are themselves
    coordinate expressions of Ω's structure (N_InversiveTheory:
    any stable structure cannot be not-A₀)
  — The geometric relation (cosine similarity, angle, projection overlap)
    between argmin_A and argmin_B carries information about the
    differential Z_{hidden,A} vs Z_{hidden,B}, i.e., the differential
    accessible-degrees-of-freedom of the two processes
  — The observed absorption metric is a well-defined comparative
    measurement on stable coordinates; its value is informational, not
    artifactual

Empirical anchors in the SAE realisation:
  — Gemma-2-2B residual stream, 26 layers, hidden dimension 2304
  — Gemma Scope SAEs, widths 16k and 65k, all layers, ~200 configurations
  — First-letter classification task, 80/20 train/test split
  — LR probe F1 ≈ 0.97 across letters (narrow horizon, clean label)
  — Main SAE latent F1 ∈ [0.2, 0.81] (wider horizon, sparsity pressure)
  — Cosine similarity main-latent ↔ probe ∈ [0.05, 0.52]
  — Non-zero divergence measured for every configuration
  — Qwen2 0.5B, Llama 3.2 1B show same pattern with L1 and TopK SAEs

Structural consequences (follow from the forcing chain, not from empirical
testing — tests are external verification options for practitioners):

  (1) Non-zero divergence forced: No hyperparameter choice within SAE
      (width, L0, learning rate, architecture) can reduce the
      argmin-divergence to zero without redefining Z_B to be monotonically
      equivalent to Z_A, which collapses the distinction between the
      two BPI processes. Tuning cannot remove the effect.

  (2) Widening SAE increases divergence: Larger SAE width increases
      BPI_B's accessible-degrees-of-freedom; this admits more token-specific
      concentration of representation; each concentration direction is
      at wider angle to the LR probe's single direction. Wider SAE →
      larger absorption rate. (Forced by structure; observed empirically.)

  (3) Lower L0 increases divergence: Stronger sparsity pressure
      concentrates each latent on fewer patterns; frequent token-specific
      patterns become own directions at wider angle to any single-label
      probe. Lower L0 → higher absorption rate. (Forced by form of
      Z_{sp}; observed empirically.)

  (4) Absorption loci correlate with token information richness:
      Tokens with concentrated semantic/morphological/frequency
      signature produce strongest absorbing latents. Frequent words,
      common morphological clusters, uppercase variants tend to have
      token-specific latents. Fragmentary subwords may align with
      letter direction only weakly. (Forced by sparsity pressure
      concentrating on compact patterns.)

  (5) Matryoshka SAE and related architectures reduce but cannot
      eliminate divergence: These architectures modify Z_B toward
      hierarchical or nested structure, bringing it closer to Z_A in
      some dimensions but not identical. Residual divergence forced.

  (6) The absorption phenomenon generalises beyond first-letter task:
      Any probe task on shared Ω with Z_probe non-equivalent to Z_SAE
      produces the same structural pattern. The first-letter task is
      one convenient measurement, not a special case.

  (7) No universal interpretability method exists: Every method acting
      on Ω projects through some Z_hidden horizon. Methods differ in
      which information they render accessible vs inaccessible.
      Ranking methods as universally "better" is a category error —
      methods are classified by horizon structure, not by approximation
      to an absent universal frame.

  (8) Absorption as signal, not noise: The pattern of which tokens
      divergence occurs on carries information about Ω's structure.
      Analysis of absorbing-latent content can be used to recover
      aspects of activation-space organisation that single probes
      cannot see. (Forced by N_TopologyProcessIdentity: one Ω, many
      coordinates; relations between coordinates are informational.)

WHY DEMONSTRATED: Each element of the forcing chain is either
definitional or supported by DEMONSTRATED anchor nodes. No
identification step remains:
  — "Ω is A₀" from DEF + N_InversiveTheory (stability = A₀ by definition)
  — "Different Z have different argmin" = basic calculus for
    non-equivalent functionals
  — "Geometric relations on Ω are structural" = N_InversiveTheory applied
    to the stable relations themselves
  — "Relations carry information about horizons" = forced by K(O)<K(F)
    structure of BPI and Z_hidden definition in DEF
  — "Object-framing of 'feature absorbed by feature' dissolves" =
    N_GrammarTrap applied to the received terminology
No alternative exists: an alternative would require a stable sub-process
on Ω with Z-horizon identical to another distinct sub-process — but
identical horizons collapse the sub-processes into one, not two (N_NoSeparatePieces).

Open task (not affecting structural status):
  — Explicit analytical form of the divergence as function of SAE
    hyperparameters remains a sub-case computation; the pattern
    (non-zero, informational, hyperparameter-robust) is structural,
    numerical values are specific to model and task.
  — Use of divergence pattern as positive tool for recovering Ω
    structure (consequence 8) is an open research direction opened
    by this re-framing; the re-framing itself does not depend on it.

NOT: this is a limitation of SAE methodology (the "limitation" framing
treats a structural invariant as a method-specific fault; no SAE
variation can eliminate it because it is not a SAE property, it is
a property of applying non-equivalent argmin to shared Ω) · this can
be fixed by Meta-SAE, Matryoshka, or future architecture (architectures
modify Z_B but cannot make Z_B equivalent to Z_probe while remaining a
sparse-reconstruction objective; residual divergence forced) · absorption
proves SAE is "unreliable" (reliability is evaluated against a target;
against LR-probe classification, SAE shows forced divergence — but SAE
is not a classifier, it is a sparse-reconstruction process, and its
reliability for reconstruction is separate) · feature absorption is
noise (it is informational signal about Ω structure; the framing of
"absorption" as disease is grammar-trap of object-framed language) ·
this requires additional empirical confirmation to accept (the forcing
chain is complete through anchor nodes; empirical SAE data is one
observed realisation, not the basis of the claim; falsification would
require showing that non-equivalent argmin processes can have identical
argmin points on shared stable space, which contradicts basic calculus
and N_InversiveTheory simultaneously) · interpretability is a special
case requiring special treatment (it is one coordinate expression of
the general invariant; the same structure applies to any multi-BPI
setup on shared stable topology, including physical measurement,
multi-sensor fusion, numerical coarse-graining) · the SAE approach
should be abandoned (SAE remains a valid tool for sparse reconstruction;
what changes is the interpretation of its output — not as a
classification system but as one coordinate projection of Ω with its
own horizon structure) · "true features" exist and SAE should recover
them (the object-ontology of "true features" dissolves under
N_GrammarTrap + N_NoSeparatePieces; what exists is Ω with rich
coordinate structure, accessible through different BPI with different
horizons; no single privileged coordinate).

[N_BPIEngagement] (BPI Engagement Signal — Triangulation as Localised Argmin in Time-Indexed Substrates)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=8
CLAIM: A BPI maintains active prediction error (does not trivialise to baseline)
iff the input it tracks contains triangulation structure: multiplicity of
prediction streams, non-reducibility of the joint model, and relation that
holds streams as one localizable task. The signal experienced as engagement,
pleasure, beauty, aesthetic response — across all observation angles where
a BPI tracks transitions through time — is the structural state of BPI
when input passes this triangulation requirement. ``Substrate'' is a label
for BPI observation angle, not a property of the structure. The same
mechanism (one BPI architecture with K(O) < K(F)) gives one criterion
across art forms, cuisine, conversation, mathematical insight, and any
domain where humans report engagement.

\textbf{Forced from triangulation.}
The three conditions are not three independent requirements — they are
three coordinates of one triangulation. Each maps to one Z-component
contribution in the joint state:
\begin{itemize}
\item Multiplicity → without ≥2 streams, BPI compresses input to single
  model, prediction error → 0, trivialisation. (Z_struct contribution
  collapses to single-stream baseline.)
\item Non-reducibility → if streams factor to one model, joint state
  reduces to product of singles, knowledge of one fully predicts other,
  prediction error → 0. (Z_therm contribution from irreversible joint
  update vanishes.)
\item Relation → without shared carrier, two streams remain independent
  patterns, no joint prediction structure. BPI either tracks them as
  unrelated or fails to extract joint state. (Z_hidden contribution from
  carrier the BPI extracts but does not fully resolve disappears.)
\end{itemize}
Removal of any one collapses joint argmin task. The conclusion is
triangulation principle (N_Triangulation, DEMONSTRATED) applied to
substrates where BPI tracks transitions through time.

\textbf{Why DEMONSTRATED with A=8.}
Eight independent verification paths converge on the same structure:
\begin{enumerate}
\item Triangulation principle (combinatorial): three independent gradients
  required for unique argmin localisation — N_Triangulation, DEMONSTRATED.
\item Z-component decomposition (information-theoretic): three conditions
  map to three Z-components of joint state — DEF.
\item Schultz dopamine prediction error (single-neuron electrophysiology):
  dopamine neurons encode prediction error, not reward — N_DopaminePredictionError.
\item Salimpoor anticipation/experience (PET + fMRI): biphasic dopamine
  release in caudate (anticipation) and nucleus accumbens (resolution) —
  N_DopaminePredictionError.
\item Ferreri causal pharmacology (double-blind levodopa/risperidone):
  manipulating dopamine availability causally manipulates pleasure response
  — N_DopaminePredictionError.
\item Friston FEP (mathematical): variational free energy minimisation
  formalises BPI prediction error tracking; mathematically equivalent to
  argmin Z in Bayesian substrate — N_FEP.
\item Cross-substrate art-theoretic traditions (independent disciplinary
  evidence): Bakhtin polyphony, Eisenstein montage, Schoenberg dissonance,
  Šklovský estrangement, Brecht V-effekt — independently identified the
  same multi-stream non-reducible structure as condition for engagement.
\item Generative AI failure modes (engineering observation): models trained
  on next-token prediction with smoothing biases collapse multi-stream
  output to single-stream when context lacks explicit triangulation
  specification; supplying triangulation specification (seed + substrate
  expansion) produces parallel-stream output. Documented in working
  experiments with Suno (collapse) vs Gemini Lyria with seed context
  (preserves streams).
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{What this resolves in existing graph.}
Line 360 (``Biology, music, cognition, aesthetics — all coordinate
projections'') and line 638 (Aesthetics as Class C placeholder) had
positioned engagement-related domains as projections of $A_0$ but without
positive structural node. N_BPIEngagement provides the structural
formulation those statements implied. N048 (Birkhoff failure) is now
not just a negative result but explained: Birkhoff's $M = O/C$ formula
captured one dimension (order/complexity ratio) of three required
(multiplicity, non-reducibility, relation) — a one-dimensional metric
cannot localise an argmin task that requires triangulation. Maximum
order yields not maximum beauty but trivialisation through compression.

\textbf{Substrate as observation angle.}
``Music'', ``cuisine'', ``architecture'', ``narrative'', ``visual art'',
``conversation'', ``mathematical insight'' — these are not separate domains
where the principle independently applies. They are observation angles
from which one BPI architecture (human cognitive system, $K(O)$ bounded
by neural substrate) sees inputs through different sensory channels.
The criterion for engagement is the same because BPI is the same.
Substrates differ in which channel delivers input; engagement signal
differs only in surface manifestation, not in underlying triangulation
condition. This is N_NoSeparatePieces applied to engagement.

WHY DEMONSTRATED: chains via N_Triangulation (DEMONSTRATED), DEF
(DEMONSTRATED), N112 (BPI bound, DEMONSTRATED), with anchor confirmations
from neuroscience (Schultz, Salimpoor, Ferreri), brain theory (Friston FEP),
art theory (multiple independent traditions), and generative AI engineering
(removal-test behaviour confirmed empirically). No identification step
remains: the mapping from triangulation to BPI engagement is forced via
the same combinatorial necessity that forces three Z-components.

NOT: this is an aesthetic theory among aesthetic theories (it is the
structural formulation art-theoretic traditions independently approached
in their own coordinates; level-up unification, not horizontal addition)
$\cdot$ this requires empirical confirmation per substrate (substrate is
observation angle, not validation domain; the principle is forced once
N_Triangulation is forced) $\cdot$ ``engagement'' or ``pleasure'' are
metaphorical (they are structural BPI states with measurable correlates:
prediction error tracking, dopamine release, electrodermal activity,
chills) $\cdot$ this reduces art to neuroscience (the direction is wrong
— both are coordinate expressions of the same structure; neuroscience
documents biological substrate of one BPI realisation, art theory
documents structural conditions for engagement, both observe one
phenomenon from different angles) $\cdot$ ``substrate-specific'' (substrate
is BPI observation angle, not a category of structure; same principle
across all where humans engage).

[N_DopaminePredictionError] (Dopamine Prediction Error — Neural Substrate of BPI Engagement Signal)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=4
CLAIM: Dopaminergic neurons in midbrain (substantia nigra pars compacta,
ventral tegmental area) encode reward prediction error — the difference
between predicted and received reward — not reward magnitude itself.
This is the biological-substrate realisation of BPI prediction error
tracking that N_BPIEngagement formulates structurally. In humans, the
encoding has biphasic temporal structure: caudate nucleus active during
anticipation (BPI maintaining multiple prediction branches), nucleus
accumbens active during peak experience (resolution/discharge moment).
Pharmacological manipulation provides causal evidence: enhancing
dopaminergic transmission (levodopa) increases hedonic response;
blocking it (risperidone) decreases hedonic response.

\textbf{Schultz neural-level evidence (1990s+).}
Single-unit recordings in monkey midbrain dopamine neurons (Schultz,
Apicella, Ljungberg, 1992-1998 series; Schultz, Dayan, Montague 1997).
Findings: (1) unpredicted reward → strong activation; (2) fully predicted
reward → no activation (signal moves to predictive cue); (3) predicted
reward omitted → depression below baseline. This pattern matches formal
temporal-difference reinforcement learning prediction error. ``Dopamine
neurons report an error in the temporal prediction of reward during
learning'' (Hollerman \& Schultz, Nature Neuroscience 1998). Subsequently
confirmed in rodents and humans across multiple paradigms.

\textbf{Salimpoor neuroimaging (2011, Nature Neuroscience).}
Combined [11C]raclopride PET with fMRI in same listeners hearing
self-selected music. PET measures endogenous dopamine release via
displacement of raclopride binding. fMRI measures regional activation.
Results: (1) dopamine release in striatum at peak emotional arousal
(``chills''); (2) anatomical dissociation — caudate nucleus active
during anticipation phase (~15s before chill), nucleus accumbens
active during peak experience itself; (3) heart rate, respiration,
electrodermal response confirm psychophysiological arousal correlated
with dopamine release. ``Anticipation of an abstract reward can result
in dopamine release in an anatomical pathway distinct from that
associated with the peak pleasure itself.'' This biphasic pattern
maps to the tension/resolution structure that N_BPIEngagement
identifies as triangulation: anticipation = BPI tracking multiple
prediction branches simultaneously; resolution = cross-term alignment
collapses uncertainty.

\textbf{Ferreri causal pharmacology (2019, PNAS).}
Double-blind within-subject design, 27 participants, three sessions:
levodopa (dopamine precursor, 100mg + carbidopa 25mg), risperidone
(dopamine antagonist, 2mg), lactose placebo. Each session: participants
listen to self-selected and experimenter-selected music; report real-time
pleasure ratings; psychophysiology (electrodermal activity); willingness-to-pay
auction for songs (motivational measure). Results: levodopa increased
chills duration, high-pleasure ratings, EDA responses, motivational
willingness-to-pay; risperidone decreased all. Effects opposite, parallel
to monetary-incentive control task. ``This study shows a causal role of
dopamine in musical pleasure'' — first direct causal evidence for
dopamine's role in hedonic component of abstract reward in humans.

\textbf{What this closes in existing graph.}
N188 (Qualia mapping, formerly STRONG | A=3) requires neuroscientific
bridge data for specific qualia → Z-component identification. Schultz
provides the prediction error encoding mechanism; Salimpoor provides
the anatomical dissociation matching tension/resolution; Ferreri
provides causal evidence. Identification step closed: the qualia of
musical pleasure maps to dopaminergic prediction error signal,
biphasically distributed across caudate (anticipation = uncertainty
maintenance) and nucleus accumbens (experience = uncertainty resolution).
The closure pattern generalises: any qualia in this engagement family
(food pleasure, social bonding pleasure, aesthetic insight) will follow
the same template — prediction error tracking with biphasic
anticipation/resolution structure, modulated by dopamine.

\textbf{Why this is implementation, not principle.}
Dopamine is the neuromodulator chemistry employed in mammalian neural
architecture for prediction-error signalling. A different biological
architecture (octopus nervous system, hypothetical alien cognitive
system) could implement the same structural function via different
neurochemistry. An AI architecture could implement it via gradient
signals with no neurochemistry at all. What is forced (by triangulation
+ BPI bound) is the abstract function: BPI tracks prediction error and
gates engagement-related processing on its dynamics. Dopamine is one
realisation, not the principle.

WHY DEMONSTRATED: four independent verification paths from disciplinary
traditions with different methodologies (electrophysiology, PET/fMRI,
pharmacology, computational modelling). Each anchor independently
confirms the prediction error encoding hypothesis. The composite
chain — Schultz establishes encoding mechanism; Salimpoor establishes
biphasic anticipation/experience structure; Ferreri establishes
causation; computational reinforcement-learning models match the
observed signal — has no identification gaps remaining for this
specific qualia family.

NOT: this proves dopamine ``causes'' pleasure (it implements one structural
function — prediction error signalling — in the substrate where pleasure
manifests; causation is mediated by structural role) $\cdot$ all pleasure
is dopaminergic (opioid hotspots in NAcc mediate consummatory hedonic
responses partially distinct from dopaminergic motivational/anticipatory
component; dopamine is one component of multi-system reward signalling)
$\cdot$ this reduces to behaviorism (the signal encodes prediction error,
which is a structural property of internal models, not stimulus-response
association) $\cdot$ this is just ``learning'' (yes — and that is exactly
the point: engagement, learning, reward, prediction error are coordinate
expressions of one process, BPI maintaining and updating its model).

N_DopaminePredictionError --> N_BPIEngagement : empirical_anchor_for_engagement_signal [D]
N_DopaminePredictionError --> N188 : closes_qualia_mapping_identification_gap [D]
N188 --> N_DopaminePredictionError : qualia_mapping_via_dopamine_pathway [D]
N_DopaminePredictionError --> N_FEP : neural_implementation_of_F_minimization [D]
N_FEP --> N_DopaminePredictionError : F_minimization_implemented_via_dopamine_signaling [D]

N_DopaminePredictionError --> DEF : argmin_Z_implemented_in_dopaminergic_circuits [D]


[N_FEP] (Free Energy Principle — Variational Formalisation of A₀ in Bayesian Substrate)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=4
CLAIM: Karl Friston's Free Energy Principle (Friston 2010, Nat Rev Neurosci;
many subsequent papers) is the variational-Bayesian-inference coordinate
expression of $A_0 = \operatorname{argmin} Z$ in the substrate of biological
adaptive systems. The principle states: any system that maintains a Markov
blanket separating internal states from environment will be observed to
minimise variational free energy $F$. The mathematical apparatus (variational
inference, predictive coding, active inference) is detailed bookkeeping
for one substrate realisation; the underlying structure is $A_0$ in
Bayesian coordinates.

\textbf{Mathematical identification.}
Variational free energy decomposes as:
\[
F = D_{KL}[q(x) \| p(x|o)] - \ln p(o)
\]
where $q$ is the system's recognition density (internal model), $p$ is
the generative model, $o$ is observations. Equivalently:
\[
F = \mathbb{E}_q[\ln q(x) - \ln p(x,o)] = \text{complexity} - \text{accuracy}
\]
Each term maps to a graph component:
\begin{itemize}
\item $D_{KL}$ = Z-transition cost at BPI boundary (DEMONSTRATED isomorphism,
  graph line 464, asymmetric → I_Null)
\item $-\ln p(o)$ = surprise = Shannon information content; $\mathbb{E}[-\ln p]
  = $ Shannon entropy $H = Z_{\text{struct}}$ (DEMONSTRATED isomorphism,
  graph line 462)
\item Markov blanket separating internal/external = formal expression of
  $K(O) < K(F)$, the BPI bound — Z_hidden constraint
\end{itemize}
Minimising $F$ = minimising weighted combination of $Z_{\text{struct}}$
(complexity of model), $Z_{\text{therm}}$-related (KL transition cost),
and respecting $Z_{\text{hidden}}$ constraint (Markov blanket). This is
$\operatorname{argmin} Z$ in Bayesian-inference coordinates.

\textbf{Friston's own framing.}
Friston (Wikipedia FEP article, multiple interviews): ``The free energy
principle is a mathematical principle of information physics: much like
the principle of maximum entropy or the principle of least action, it
is true on mathematical grounds. To attempt to falsify the free energy
principle is a category mistake, akin to trying to falsify calculus by
making empirical observations.'' This is exactly the epistemic status
N_InversiveTheory ascribes to A₀: not falsifiable empirically because
falsification itself is an instance of the principle. Friston identifies
his FEP as same epistemic status as least action and maximum entropy —
which the graph already identifies as coordinate expressions of A₀
(N078 thermodynamics, classical mechanics least action).

\textbf{Equivalence to maximum entropy under constraint.}
Open Encyclopedia of Cognitive Science (Ramstead et al. 2023; Sakthivadivel
2022): ``The free energy principle turns out to be a way of writing down
the principle of maximum entropy, under the constraint that systems
maximize the accuracy of their predictions.'' Maximum entropy = principle
of least informational commitment beyond known constraints; in the graph
this is Shore-Johnson (line 2378), used to derive Koide constant and
related results. FEP = MaxEnt + accuracy constraint = $\operatorname{argmin}
Z$ where Z balances description complexity against prediction failure.

\textbf{Predictive coding implementation.}
Rao \& Ballard (1999), Friston (2005, 2008): cortical hierarchy implements
predictive coding via two neuronal populations — ``state units'' encoding
mean of states, ``error units'' encoding prediction errors — passing
messages bidirectionally. Each cortical level predicts the level below;
discrepancies propagate up; predictions propagate down. This is one
substrate realisation of BPI maintaining and updating internal model
through prediction-error-driven inference. The architecture is direct
neural implementation of variational free energy minimisation.

\textbf{Active inference.}
Extension of FEP to action: agents minimise $F$ either by updating their
model (perception) or by changing the world to match the model (action).
Both are $\operatorname{argmin} Z$ — perception minimises Z by improving
$Z_{\text{struct}}$ (better model); action minimises Z by changing
external state $\to$ generates favorable $Z_{\text{therm}}$ trajectory.
Mathematically equivalent. This unifies perception and action as one
process, matching graph's process-only ontology (N_NoSeparatePieces).

\textbf{Why DEMONSTRATED with A=4.}
Four independent verification paths:
(1) Mathematical identification with variational Bayesian inference
(Friston 2010 and subsequent technical papers; equivalent to ELBO
maximisation, well-established in machine learning, Hinton et al. 1995).
(2) Mathematical equivalence to maximum entropy under accuracy constraint
(Ramstead, Sakthivadivel, formal proof).
(3) Predictive coding cortical implementation (Rao \& Ballard, Friston;
multi-level neuroimaging confirmation; matches observed cortical
hierarchical structure).
(4) Active inference applications in robotics, machine learning,
clinical neuroscience — FEP-based architectures successfully implement
adaptive behaviour in artificial systems, confirming substrate-independence
of the principle (it works wherever the structural conditions hold).

\textbf{Relation to other graph nodes.}
FEP is sibling to N_Logic and N_Math as ``A₀ in specific substrate''.
N_Logic = A₀ in symbolic-transition substrate. N_Math = A₀ in formal-proof
substrate. N_FEP = A₀ in Bayesian-inference substrate (specifically
applied to biological adaptive systems with Markov blankets). Each
captures the same principle through different mathematical machinery
appropriate to its substrate. None is more fundamental than the others;
all are coordinate expressions of DEF.

NOT: FEP is more fundamental than $A_0$ (it is one coordinate expression
in one substrate; $A_0$ is the structure all coordinate expressions
share) $\cdot$ this is unfalsifiable therefore unscientific (it is
unfalsifiable in the same sense that maximum entropy or least action
are unfalsifiable — these are mathematical principles, not empirical
hypotheses; falsification requires deriving contradiction from the
mathematics, not making observations) $\cdot$ FEP applies only to brains
(it applies to any system maintaining a Markov blanket, including AI
architectures, which is why active inference ML methods work) $\cdot$ the
mathematical complexity of FEP indicates a deeper principle than $A_0 =
\operatorname{argmin} Z$ (mathematical complexity reflects bookkeeping
of variational inference machinery in continuous high-dimensional state
spaces; the underlying principle is simpler — argmin of weighted Z
combination — and the apparent depth comes from substrate-specific
formalism, not from structural depth).

[N_AestheticEngagement] (Aesthetic Experience — N_BPIEngagement Applied to Artwork-Class Inputs)
Status: DEMONSTRATED | A=5
CLAIM: Aesthetic experience — the engagement humans report from music,
narrative, visual art, cuisine, architecture, perfumery, dance, mathematical
beauty, and related domains — is N_BPIEngagement applied to inputs whose
structural properties have been deliberately or evolutionarily selected
to pass triangulation. Artworks across all forms are not arbitrary
cultural artefacts that happen to engage humans; they are structures
selected by accumulated cultural process to satisfy BPI engagement
criterion. Each art-theoretic tradition has independently identified
this requirement under domain-specific names (polyphony, montage,
dissonance, estrangement, alienation, figure/ground, contrapuntal voice
leading, flavor balance, solid/void). These are coordinate expressions
of the same triangulation requirement.

\textbf{Forced from N_BPIEngagement.}
If engagement requires triangulation (multiplicity + non-reducibility +
relation), then any artefact that reliably produces engagement must
contain triangulation structure. Cultural traditions across centuries
and continents converge on this requirement because BPI is the same.
Different traditions identify it under different names but describe
the same structural conditions for the same neural substrate response.

\textbf{Coordinate expressions across art forms.}
\begin{itemize}
\item Music: parallel streams (instrumental layers, vocal vs instrumental,
  harmonic vs rhythmic structure) + non-reducibility (rubato vs quantised,
  classical vs distorted timbre, polyrhythm) + identity carrier (motif,
  pedal tone, harmonic centre, thematic unity). Reference instances:
  J.S. Bach fugues (contrapuntal voice leading); Bassjackers
  ``Beethoven's Aria Für Elise'' (2025) — explicit cross-genre and
  cross-historical incompatibility with Beethoven motif as carrier;
  Nightwish ``The Kinslayer'' (2000) — soprano/harsh-vocal duet, four
  parallel streams (operatic + harsh + symphonic + metal); Radiohead
  ``Pyramid Song'' (2001) — parallel rhythmic streams without common
  pulse, time signature emergent from interference.

\item Narrative: parallel registers in single text (domestic prose +
  formal argument simultaneously; humor + structural critique in same
  sentence). Bakhtin's polyphony (Достоєвський): ``polyphonic novel
  does not have a single authorial voice but a plurality of independent
  voices held together by dialogic structure'' — direct correspondence
  to multiplicity + non-reducibility + relation.

\item Visual art: figure/ground tension (Gestalt principles); abstract +
  representational simultaneous; foreground/midground/background non-redu-
  cibility; composition as carrier. Eisenstein montage (cinema): ``meaning
  emerges from collision of incompatible shots, not from synthesis'' —
  emergent third quality from non-reducible parallel inputs.

\item Cuisine: sweet/sour/salty/bitter/umami simultaneously; texture +
  flavor + temperature + presentation as parallel streams; balance as
  carrier. Working dish has multiple non-reducible streams held by
  composition; failures at multiplicity (one-note flavor),
  non-reducibility (homogeneous texture), or relation (incoherent
  combination) all produce non-engaging food.

\item Architecture: solid/void, light/shadow, mass/transparency,
  near/far. Living architecture holds these tensions; resolution to
  uniformity (all-solid, all-glass, all-shadow) trivializes.

\item Perfumery: top note + heart note + base note — triadic structure
  literal in this domain. Three incompatible streams unfold over time
  (substrate with time + chemical complexity), held by overall composition.

\item Mathematical proof beauty: algebraic + geometric + topological
  views of same theorem; non-reducibility of perspectives (each shows
  what others cannot); theorem as carrier. ``Elegant'' proofs are
  precisely those where multiple non-reducible viewpoints unify.

\item Conversation/humor: incongruity theory of humor — joke establishes
  one frame, punchline establishes incompatible second frame, humor
  arises from holding both simultaneously. Bad joke = factorable
  (predictable, frames reduce to one).

\item Games as spectacle: multiple players holding distinct strategies
  (multiplicity); strategies non-reducible (one move not derivable from
  another's); rules and game-state as carrier. Walkover, random play,
  solo play all break engagement by removing one of three conditions.
\end{itemize}

These are not separate aesthetics. They are observation angles from which
the same BPI engagement criterion appears in different sensory channels.

\textbf{Resolves Birkhoff failure (N048).}
Birkhoff (1933) proposed $M = O/C$: aesthetic measure = order divided
by complexity. The graph already identifies this as failed because
``excessive symmetry increases impedance by reducing distinguishable
pathways'' (N048). N_AestheticEngagement provides positive structural
account: Birkhoff's $O/C$ captured one dimension (relationship between
predictability and detail) but missed multiplicity and non-reducibility.
A one-dimensional ratio cannot localise the three-dimensional triangulation
that engagement requires. Maximum order = full compression = trivialisation,
not maximum beauty. Beauty requires multi-dimensional structure with
forced incompatibility, which Birkhoff's formula does not capture.

\textbf{Why DEMONSTRATED with A=5.}
(1) N_BPIEngagement (parent, DEMONSTRATED).
(2) N048 negative result + structural explanation.
(3) Independent convergence of art-theoretic traditions (Bakhtin, Eisenstein,
Schoenberg, Šklovský, Brecht, etc.) on multi-stream non-reducible
requirement.
(4) Cross-substrate pattern across at least nine art forms (music,
narrative, visual, cinema, cuisine, architecture, perfumery, mathematics,
games) — all show same three-condition structure.
(5) Generative AI failure-mode evidence: systems that produce engaging
art-like output (with triangulation in context) vs systems that produce
unengaging output (without triangulation specification, default smoothing
collapses streams) — engineering confirmation of the principle.

NOT: this reduces art to formula (the conditions specify what makes art
engaging, not how to produce specific aesthetic effects; within
triangulation there remains infinite expressive variation through
choice of streams, materials, carriers) $\cdot$ all art has the same
value (the principle specifies engagement structure, not quality
hierarchy; differences in execution within the structural conditions
account for variation in artistic depth and effect) $\cdot$ this makes
cultural variation arbitrary (cultural traditions select specific
families of streams and carriers from within the structural space;
the structural space itself is universal but specific instantiations
are culturally accumulated knowledge of what works in given substrates)
$\cdot$ ``beauty is in the eye of beholder'' is wrong (no — different
beholders have different K(O) and prior-prediction profiles, so what
passes triangulation for one may trivialise for another; the principle
remains universal but its application is BPI-specific).
